## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / mathematical biology (population dynamics ODEs)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is the time-derivative of population size P, indicating a deterministic population growth model (ordinary differential equation) where growth depends on current population (density dependence) and possibly explicit time forcing t (seasonality, changing resources, interventions).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited resources, per-capita rate constant)
- Linear time-varying per-capita rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P (gradual environmental improvement/decline)
- Density-dependent (logistic differential form): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (carrying capacity with c1 тЙИ 1/K)
- Logistic expanded polynomial: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (same mechanism as logistic; easier for regression)
- Theta-logistic (generalized crowding): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (nonlinear density dependence; c2 controls crowding steepness)
- Gompertz growth (log-density regulation): dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 * P**(-1)) (per-capita growth decreases with log(P))
- Allee effect (critical population threshold): dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 * P - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (negative growth at low P; saturation at high P)
- Constant immigration/emigration: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 (net influx/outflux independent of P)
- Proportional harvesting/mortality: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (removal rate proportional to population)
- Nonlinear harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P**c3 (effort or predation scaling nonlinearly with P)
- Beverton-Holt-type saturation in births: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (births saturate at high P; linear deaths)
- Seasonally forced growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t + c4)) (periodic environment/resource availability)
- Time-varying carrying capacity (via time-varying 1/K): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * (1 + c2 * exp(-c3 * t))) (resources/carrying capacity shifts over time)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Per-capita growth approximately constant тЖТ dP_dt proportional to P (pure exponential regime at low density).
- Crowding/competition limiting resources тЖТ negative curvature in dP_dt vs P, often captured by a -P**2 term or a (1 - c*P) factor.
- Sharper-than-logistic density dependence (e.g., strong territoriality) тЖТ higher-order crowding such as (1 - (c*P)**theta).
- Presence of a critical minimum viable population (mate limitation/cooperation) тЖТ Allee structure with a low-P zero crossing (factor like (c*P - 1)).
- Birth processes saturating with density (limited nesting sites) тЖТ rational birth term P/(1 + c*P) rather than polynomial decline.
- External additions/removals not tied to P (stocking, constant migration) тЖТ additive constant term in dP_dt.
- Management/predation proportional to available individuals тЖТ subtractive term proportional to P; disproportionate capture/predation тЖТ subtractive P**c term.
- Seasonality or cyclic climate тЖТ multiplicative sinusoidal modulation in time, often multiplying the baseline growth term.
- Gradual regime shift (habitat restoration or deterioration) тЖТ time-varying coefficients via exp(-c*t) or low-order polynomials in t.
